Police Attorney Detailed the Kidnapping and Case-Solving Process

Victim Injured and Unable to Attend, Four Kidnappers Detained Pending Further Interrogation

Wang Boying (also known as Boyin), the manager of the Damai Qianzhuang and director of the Dadong Bookstore, a Shaoxing native, was kidnapped on the night of the 9th of this month at 11:40 PM along with his concubine, Madam Wang Li, while riding in his private car, number 5321. As soon as they reached the entrance of Lane 102, Changfeng Lane, on Tongfu Road, they encountered three kidnappers, two men and one woman, who boarded the car with weapons, forced out Madam Li, and drove Wang and the car away. They sent a letter to the family demanding a ransom of 200,000 yuan, a truly shocking amount. After Wang's family reported the incident to the police, the Chengdu Road Police Department, led by Chinese Detective Feng Baishun, Detectives Cui Chengke and Yang Xinzheng, Senior Detectives Huang Fuson and Xu Dezhong, and Western Detectives, apprehended the kidnapper Wang Liugen, a local, and his suspected accomplice, Wang Cai, in room 201 of the Dafang Hotel on Zhengjia Muqiao Street. They confiscated a handgun. Based on Wang's confession, they, along with detectives from the French Concession Police Department, went to the hideout at No. 14 Rongfu Lane, Xiai Ansi Road, to arrest accomplices. Yao Maoqing, the kidnapper guarding the victim, refused to open the door and was shot and killed by the detectives. Stray bullets injured Wang Boying's arm, and the victim was rescued. They also confiscated a Mauser pistol. They then went to room 306 of the Dazhong Hotel and apprehended Yang Kong, Wang's nanny, a Liyang native, and Wang's three-year-old son. They also apprehended Zhang Zhengguo, a Yangzhou native, an accomplice, at the intersection of Yapei Road and Fuxu Road. The body of the deceased was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for examination by the Second Special District Court, and the other four kidnappers, along with the weapons, were returned to the police station and detained separately. Details have already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police sent the four kidnappers to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special District Court, where Judge Liu Yugui presided over the interrogation. The defendant Zhang Zhengguo hired lawyer Wu Linkun for his defense. The details of the trial are recorded below.

Details of the Kidnapping

Police attorney Zhang Tianyin began by detailing the events, stating that the victim, Wang Boying, resides at No. 3 Guiren Lane, Lane 195, Maigen Road, and is a director of the Dadong Bookstore. His concubine, Madam Li, resides at No. 19, Changfeng Lane, Lane 102, Tongfu Road. On the evening of the 9th of this month, Wang had dinner at his concubine's residence. At approximately 7:00 PM, he telephoned his wife's residence and asked her to have the car driven over. The car's number was 5321. At 11:00 PM, Wang and his concubine, Madam Li, boarded the car to go to a friend surnamed Zhang on Baker Road. As the car left the lane entrance, a kidnapper (the deceased) stood in front of the car and was almost run over. Wang scolded the driver for being careless.

Ransom of 200,000

Unexpectedly, in a flash, the kidnapper and another kidnapper (Wang Liugen) boarded the car from either side, threatening them with handguns. They forced Madam Li out, and another female kidnapper (Wang Cai) also boarded the car. The deceased and Wang Cai sat on either side of Wang, and the kidnappers watched the driver and drove the car forward at high speed. When they reached Lafayette Road and Muirhead Road, they drove the driver out of the car and drove west, disappearing without a trace. Later, Wang's family reported the incident to the police. On the 11th, they received a letter from the kidnappers, which included a letter written by the victim himself, asking his parents to raise funds. The kidnappers demanded a ransom of 200,000 yuan. The kidnappers learned that Yin Zhibai, who lived at No. 9 Guiren Lane, was a person who could help, so they sent the letter directly to Yin.

Negotiations

On the 13th, Wang Gumei, who lived at No. 10 Guiren Lane, also received a letter from the victim, also asking her to help. She reported the letter to the police, and Wang's family sent representatives, Xiao Chan, along with Detectives Cui Chengke and Huang Fuson, to negotiate with the kidnappers. They agreed to meet at 10:00 AM yesterday morning in room 201 of the Dafang Hotel to negotiate. At noon yesterday, the Chinese and Western detectives apprehended Wang Liugen and Wang Cai in the room. They found a handgun and nine bullets on Wang Cai's person. The room was registered under Wang Cai's name, who was using the alias He Xiuying. Later, at room 306 of the Dazhong Hotel, they apprehended Yang Kong and the three-year-old boy. Yang Kong claimed that she was employed by Wang as a nanny and that the child was Wang's son.

A Fierce Gunfight

Later, Wang and his wife revealed that the victim was being held at No. 14 Rongfu Lane, Lane 8, Xiai Ansi Road. The police accompanied Wang Liugen to the hideout. Wang called out at the back door, and the kidnapper inside (the deceased) opened the door upon hearing the voice. When the kidnapper saw the detectives, he knew that he had been exposed and immediately opened fire, shooting at Western Detective Gai Zilai who was nearby. Fortunately, he missed. Another Western Detective Bai Langlin and Chinese Detective Huang Fuson immediately drew their guns and returned fire. The kidnapper, Yao Maoqing, was hit by two bullets and fell dead in the kitchen. A handgun was found near his body, containing six bullets. The body has been sent to Tongren Fuyuan Hall to await examination.

Victim Hit by Bullets

During the gunfight, the victim heard the commotion in the pavilion upstairs and climbed out of the window. However, detective Ye Dezhong did not recognize him as the victim and mistook him for an accomplice, firing six shots at him, unfortunately hitting his right arm. He has been sent to the hospital and is expected to recover in ten days, according to doctors. The detectives then entered the room and found a Mauser pistol and nine bullets inside the bed in the front building. They also found more than 200 bullets, two pairs of sunglasses, and an envelope under the bed. The handwriting on the envelope was identical to that on the letters received by Wang's family, indicating that it was written by the deceased. All the kidnappers were then taken back to the police station.

Discussing the Kidnapping

Wang confessed that Zhang Zhengguo initiated the plan. Zhang was arrested at 6:05 PM yesterday afternoon in front of the Xintong Automobile Company on Albert Road and Fuxu Road. The victim, Wang Boying, was unable to attend due to his injuries. His representatives, Chan and the driver, Cifu Tang, were present for questioning. Judge Liu questioned each defendant separately, starting with Wang Liugen. Wang Liugen confessed that he used to run the Dakang Automobile Company, so he knew how to drive. In December of last year, because he was in debt, he discussed a plan with Zhang Zhengguo at the Dacheng Apartments. Zhang mentioned that Wang Boying had repeatedly hired cars from Dakang, so he knew him and knew that Wang's family was wealthy and had potential for being kidnapped, so why not give it a try.

Details of the Execution

The next day, they rented the Dafang Hotel to continue their discussions. In addition to Wang and Zhang, the deceased Yao Maoqing was also present. They decided to carry out the kidnapping. However, because they lacked weapons, Yao volunteered to find them, as Yao had previously worked in the military and could easily obtain them. They then dispersed. Later, Yao brought a Mauser pistol and two handguns (those confiscated) and set the date for February 9th to take action. Zhang and Wang rented the hideout in advance to hide the victim, paying 90 yuan as a deposit and 25 yuan per month for rent. On the 9th, Wang, his wife Cai, and Yao went to wait on the street corner. Zhang did not go because he knew the victim. At 11:00 PM, the victim came out, and they approached him. Yao dragged the concubine out, and Wang held a gun to watch the driver.

Driven to the Hideout

Because he needed both hands to drive, he could not hold the gun and handed it over to Yao. Yao held the gun with both hands, with his wife sitting on the right and Wang Cai on the left. He drove the car straight to Rongfu Lane. Zhang came once that night, asked if the person had been brought, and then left. Wang and Yao were responsible for guarding the victim. The next day, Yao sent a letter to Wang's family demanding a ransom of 200,000 yuan. This ransom had been discussed in advance. Yang Kong was a female servant, and because it was inconvenient for her to live with them, she was placed in the Dazhong Hotel.

Framed Accusation

Zhang Zhengguo stated that the Dakang Automobile Company was opened by his father, and Wang Liugen's brother was a shareholder in the company. He introduced Wang to the company, first as a driver and then to help with bookkeeping. On May 22nd of last year, Wang Liugen forged a seal and fraudulently withdrew 5,474 yuan from the Shanghai Bank, fleeing with Cai. He reported this to the Gordon Road Police Department the next day and posted a reward notice. His lawyer, Wu Linkun, presented the newspaper and the police warrant. He continued, stating that in addition to being the junior proprietor of Dakang, he also worked as a sales representative for the Xintong Automobile Company and was a legitimate businessman. How could he be involved in this kidnapping? He was being framed by Wang Liugen, whom he was currently wanted by police.

Repeatedly Waited

Wang Cai confessed that she and Wang Liugen were lovers. Because Wang had embezzled more than 5,000 yuan from the company and could not make it up, they fled to Wuxi to avoid trouble. They lived next door to Yao Maoqing, which is how they met. When they came to Shanghai, they lived in the Dacheng Apartments. In December of last year, she heard Wang say that he had agreed with Zhang Zhengguo to carry out a kidnapping and rented the house at No. 14 Rongfu Lane. Wang paid the rent. The handguns were brought by Yao. Wang and Yao had repeatedly waited on Tongfu Road.

Detained Pending Further Interrogation

On that day, she was asked by Yao to go with him, saying, "Don't be afraid, the victim doesn't have a gun, so come with us." She went along just to observe. Unexpectedly, they took action that day. Yao stood in front of the car and dragged out the victim's concubine, sitting on either side of the victim with her. She did not hold a gun. Her husband was the driver and took the victim to Rongfu Lane. Yao was responsible for guarding. She had been there several times and acted as a guard once. Yang Kong confessed that she was a nanny and knew nothing about the kidnapping. Wang Liugen stated that Zhang was indeed an accomplice and was not being framed. Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the confessions and ordered that all the defendants be detained for seven days for further interrogation.

Examination of the Deceased Kidnapper

According to a report from the French Concession Constable, Wang Boyin, a native of Shaoxing residing at No. 17 Changfeng Lane, Tongfu Road, in the Public Concession, was kidnapped on the night of the 9th of this month and hidden in the hideout at No. 14 Rongfu Lane, Xiai Ansi Road, in the French Concession, and a large ransom was demanded. Yesterday morning, the Chengdu Road Police Department received a telephone tip that the kidnappers were negotiating the ransom at the Dafang Hotel, room 201, Zhengjia Muqiao Street, and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives, along with the French Concession Police, to apprehend two men and one woman (one of the men was the victim's representative). They also apprehended one man and one woman at the Dazhong Hotel across the street. They learned the location of the hideout and immediately rushed to rescue the victim. At that time, Yao Maoqing (25 years old), the kidnapper guarding the victim, opened fire and resisted arrest and was killed by the detectives on the spot. Details have already been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday morning, Chief Prosecutor Chen Beisan of the Second Special Court, along with medical examiner Jiang Dan and clerk Peng Ying, arrived at the mortuary to examine the body of the deceased kidnapper Yao Maoqing. One gunshot wound was found on his chest and another on his back, piercing through to the right side and the left knee. One shot hit his right hand, piercing through the palm, breaking his index finger and thumb. The medical examiner extracted one six-inch bullet each from the left side, left knee, and calf. After the examination, they took their seats. French Concession Police Constable Zhang Chunsheng reported the case. Western Detective Bao Langlige (transliteration) of the Chengdu Road Police Department testified that after they apprehended the kidnappers at the Dafang Hotel, they learned the location of the hideout and went to rescue the victim. When they arrived at the back door of the hideout, a detective knocked on the door. The deceased opened the door, and a Western detective rushed in. The deceased immediately fired two or three shots from his handgun, and he fired two shots in retaliation, and the deceased fell to the ground. Another detective fired two shots and the deceased died on the spot. They confiscated the handgun he was holding and a Mauser pistol from the bed upstairs. The female kidnapper apprehended at the Dafang Hotel also had a handgun. He requested permission to take back the bullets extracted from the body for further investigation. Chief Chen reviewed the testimony and stated that Yao Maoqing had died from gunshot wounds sustained during his lifetime and that the body could not be claimed. The two bullets extracted from the body were handed over to Western Detective Bao Langlige to be taken to the police station for further investigation. After the examination, the police took photos of the body and then sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial in coffin number 3065 in Pudong.

Group Wedding Stipulates Formal Attire Style 144

Certificate Application Deadline Extended

The group wedding organized by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, after being approved by the municipal government, is being actively prepared, and the work is extremely intense. The first wedding on April 3rd is fast approaching, so the number of people applying to register with the bureau has been very enthusiastic. The day of the ceremony is sure to be a grand occasion. Now, for the sake of uniformity, the bureau has stipulated the style of formal attire for the group wedding. The groom will wear a blue robe and a black mandarin jacket, and the bride will wear a imperial-pink cheongsam. They have already reached an agreement with the local Meiya Silk Weaving Factory to have them produce the material for the formal attire, which is made of real silk. The stipulated price for the Class A men's formal robe and jacket material is 15 yuan, and the Class B is 12 yuan. The Class A women's is five yuan, and the Class B is four yuan and two corners. The prices are all uniform. The materials will be woven by the 10th of next month. All those participating in the group wedding must wear the formal attire made by the factory. However, those who are poor and unable to afford the silk material for the formal attire can use cloth, but they must obtain the color of the formal attire from the bureau and make it in the same style to be qualified. The veil must also be rented from the factory, with a rental fee of one yuan and five corners per piece. The price of the formal attire material is stipulated to be so low to conform to the original intention of promoting economy in group weddings. In addition, the deadline for the submission of certificate styles has been formally extended to March 5th due to the fact that many of the submissions received were not suitable. The results of the solicitation will be announced on March 10th, and letters will be sent to art schools in Shanghai and other places to solicit suitable certificate styles, and generous compensation will be given. The responsible person in charge of the preparations for the event stated that there is no limit to the number of people participating in the wedding, but it will be limited to the maximum capacity of the municipal government auditorium.

Activities of the Public Works Department's Sanitation Division 145

Disease Prevention: Disinfection: Pest Control: Vaccination

The Public Works Department's Sanitation Division's activities include investigation and disinfection of infectious diseases, certification and registration of Chinese deaths, vaccination, cholera immunization, mosquito and fly control, plague prevention, inspection of licensed and other premises, investigation and handling of resident complaints, and management of public swimming pools.

Number of Vaccinations

The division administered 264,450 vaccinations last year (compared to only 181,402 in the previous year), of which 58,069 were Chinese infants or first-time vaccinators. In addition, 72,378 adults and 128,158 children were revaccinated. 3,845 foreigners were vaccinated.

Disease Prevention Immunization

During the summer, the immunization car administered 249,106 cholera immunizations. From the end of June to October, well water was disinfected with chlorine gas every week. In addition, the Waterworks Company provided free clean water to poor residents in the East and West districts, totaling 1.8 million gallons.

Mosquito Control

Mosquito control activities include house-to-house inspections, drainage of waterways, leveling of land, and application of oil to water surfaces. In addition, mosquito larvae were collected and sent to the laboratory for testing and verification. However, there is still no effective method for eliminating mosquitoes breeding in the water accumulated in the foundations of large buildings.

Fly Control

Fly control activities were carried out throughout the concession. Boric acid water was used to disinfect garbage piles. Last year, boric acid disinfection was also applied to garbage cans. In addition, fly swatting teams were dispatched from time to time to swat flies.

Swimming Pool

The admission price for the swimming pool was slightly increased last year, but the number of swimmers still exceeded 105,708 (compared to 12,140 in the previous year). The increased fee slightly reduced overcrowding and restricted undesirable elements. During the hottest period, the pool was open until 10:00 PM every day.

Statement by Butterfield & Swire Regarding Security Precautions 146

The North China Daily News reports that Butterfield & Swire issued a public notice yesterday (the 14th), stating that as a result of the investigation into the Tongzhou steamboat robbery case, several decisions have been made. First and foremost, it must be stated that the ships built for the company's inland waterway shipping operations were not designed with the specific anti-piracy features, such as protective iron railings, found on vessels operated by Butterfield & Swire in South China, where piracy is prevalent. The company is now carefully studying how to modify the interiors of ships specifically built for North China's waterways to address the piracy problem. However, it is essential to understand that the possible alterations or improvements are limited. One primary concern is that installing railings could endanger lives. This is not an overestimation, as evidenced by the case of the Liangguang (transliteration) steamboat that sank in the Gapu Water Gate (transliteration) sea channel in 1927, resulting in 135 deaths. According to the Hong Kong court coroner's inquest at the time, passengers were trapped inside the ship like rats in a rat trap, with no way to escape. In addition to studying internal modifications to the ships, Butterfield & Swire is considering and implementing other possible and convenient precautions that it has in mind or that have been suggested by the public. These include: (1) Increasing the strength of armed guards by 50%; (2) Changing the weaponry to weapons that can be used more quickly. While the Mauser pistols currently carried by the guards are undoubtedly excellent, experts believe they cannot be deployed quickly enough in an emergency. New weapons would avoid this problem; (3) Searching passengers and their luggage in each cabin before the ship weighs anchor. This search will be conducted in cooperation with the responsible authorities. It should be noted that company inspectors, both Chinese and foreign, have been conducting searches on ships for the past few years, but body searches have often angered passengers. It is now hoped that passengers can be persuaded to comply with these searches for their own benefit; (4) The ships of the two British companies operating coastal shipping in North China have begun to communicate with each other by wireless telegraphy, and the area is being managed in accordance with the British Navy's guidance in the southern piracy zone between Xiamen and Singapore. Although the intention of this measure is to enable ships to issue warnings early in case of emergencies, the primary purpose is to prevent piracy.

### Robbery Foiled, Handgun Stolen 147

Rent Collector Encountered Robbers in Pingheli

Yesterday at approximately 11:00 AM, a landlord surnamed Mou from Pingheli, Aveneu Road sent a clerk and a bodyguard to Pingheli to collect rent. As they were leaving number 40 in the neighborhood, four robbers suddenly appeared from behind, each carrying a handgun. They shouted at the rent collector and his clerk to stop. While they were struggling, Guard No. 137 from the neighborhood security office learned of the incident, and rushed to the scene with a gun. Afterward, the guard and the bodyguard, realizing that although the money had not been robbed, the gun had fallen into the robbers' hands, went together to report to the police station in charge of the area, requesting that the robbers be apprehended.

### Rickshaw Puller Robbed Intoxicated American 148

Over One Hundred Silver Dollars Stolen

Three Rickshaw Pullers Have Been Detained

An American man named Paulson, who works as a doctor on an American merchant ship, hired a rickshaw at approximately 3:00 AM on the first of this month. While traveling near Zhoushan Road and Huade Road, he was robbed by several rickshaw pullers who took advantage of his intoxication to steal a diary containing over one hundred silver dollars, worth 340 yuan, and fled without a trace. The case was reported to the Hongkou Police Station. The day before yesterday, Detective Wang Runhe received a tip from an informant and arrested three Jiangbei natives (rickshaw pullers) Chen Deshun, Wang Dingtai, and Gu Hongsheng at 122 East Broadway Road, West Huade Road, and Zhangjiaqiao in Zhabei. They were taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The lawyer Li Zhishan of the Municipal Council recounted the events, stating that the victim, Paulson, was unable to appear in court because the ship left Shanghai on the morning of the 2nd, bound for the United States. The defendants admitted at the police station that a rickshaw puller named Xiao Wang had initiated the robbery. However, they claimed that only twenty silver dollars were taken. He asked for the case to be postponed. When questioned, Chen Deshun and Wang Dingtai confessed that they each received five yuan (silver dollars) after the fact. Gu Hongsheng confessed that he received 1.60 yuan. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered that they remain in custody and set a new date for review.

### Setting Up a Anti-Drug Society to Collect Money: Huang Jiemin Approved for Transfer 149

Police Believe the Case Involves Aiding and Abetting

Yesterday, He Declared Abandonment of Appeal

Huang Jiemin from Suzhou took advantage of the authorities' strict anti-smoking campaign last year and founded the China Anti-Drug Society, establishing a national headquarters at No. 8, Sanrui Lane, Tongfu Road. He drafted a simple constitution, declaration, and fee schedule, and then went to various places to recruit people into the society as members, and instructed members to organize branch offices in various counties, districts, and townships, using the name to deceive and collect money. Although the party and government agencies successively rejected the application for registration, he still continued his activities. Recently, the Nanchang branch of the Military Affairs Commission learned that Huang Zhan dared to create a new name to swindle and cheat, and strictly ordered the local military and political authorities to instruct the Municipal Public Security Bureau to arrest him quickly. The bureau had already joined forces with the Chengdu Road Police Station to arrest Huang, along with various printed materials, seals, books, certificates, and other items, and sent them to the First Special District Court. After questioning, Huang was suspected of fraud. The court ruled to transfer him to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning. However, during the appeal period, he was temporarily detained at the police station. The relevant details have been recorded in previous reports. It is now known that the Municipal Police Department has conducted a detailed study of Huang's actions by the legal team of the Municipal Council, and has determined that since it is a case of aiding and abetting, there should be no objection. Yesterday, the lawyer in charge formally declared to the court that he would abandon the appeal, and carried out the ruling. At the same time, he notified Lawyer Zhan Jifeng, the legal advisor of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to forward the request to Director Wen, asking him to send the original investigator to the detention center to bring Huang Jiemin and the evidence back to be investigated and handled.

### Yi Fangshuo's Appeal Results in Three-Year Sentence 152

Request for Bail Denied

Yi Fangshuo, a native of Hangzhou who performed slapstick comedy at the New Company's rooftop playground, was accused of raping his cousin Yi Baozhu and his aunt Li Xiaozhen. The French Concession police arrested Yi. Later, Yi was found to have also committed the crime of buying women, Ye Jinzhu and Yang Lingzhu, and others, and making them learn drama and monitoring their actions. He was sent to the Second Special District Court for prosecution on three counts of obstructing morals, family, and freedom. During the trial, the victims withdrew their charges for obstructing morals. The court proceeded with the trial on the two counts of obstructing family and freedom. As a result, Yi Fangshuo was sentenced to three years of imprisonment for illegally depriving people of their freedom of movement. He was found not guilty of obstructing family. During the appeal period, he was transferred to the detention center to await instructions. Yi refused to accept the verdict and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Branch Court. The High Court, based on the petition, held a collegial hearing on the 8th of this month, summoned witnesses for interrogation, and announced the end of the debate, pending judgment. All the details have been recorded in the newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the date for the verdict arrived. Yi's defense lawyers Sha Xunyi and Lou Yunmei arrived at the court one after another at 2:00 PM to await instructions. Yi's wives, Yi Meimei, Yi's sisters, Yi Caitao, and relatives also arrived at the court to listen. At three o'clock, Judge Guo Dezhang, together with Assessors Sun Honglin and Jia Liang, Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, and Clerk Huang Lixiang, specially opened the Third Criminal Court to announce the verdict. Lawyer Gu Shouxi represented the Police Department and appeared in court. The two defense lawyers, Sha and Lou, also appeared in court to await the verdict. The court ordered the bailiffs to bring the appellant Yi Fangshuo from the detention center for questioning. After briefly questioning his age and origin, Judge Guo announced the main text of the verdict, that the original verdict was revoked, and that Yi Fangshuo was sentenced to one day of imprisonment for every two days of illegal detention of another person, and that he was sentenced to three years of imprisonment. After the verdict was announced, the judge briefly explained the reasons for the decision to the appellant, stating that he acknowledged that Yi had confessed that Ye Jinzhu was a maid of the Ye family, who was bought by Yi for 150 yuan to learn drama, and that he had monitored their actions. Although Ye Lishi testified in court that some had entrusted him with guardianship and some had not entrusted him with guardianship, the original trial's verdict that he had illegally deprived them of their freedom was inappropriate. Therefore, this court changed the sentence to three years of imprisonment in accordance with Article 313 of the Criminal Law, which ranges from one year to seven years of imprisonment. If he was not satisfied, he could file an appeal with the Supreme Court to this court after receiving the judgment. He was also instructed that Yi's wife, Yi Lishi, should file a petition with this court, requesting a stay of detention, on the grounds that Yi was seriously ill. This court has been handling the case until now. After observing Yi's body, there was no sign of illness. Therefore, the ruling to reject the request was made. Yi's lawyer again requested that bail be allowed during the appeal period. The court did not allow it. After the order was given, the police were ordered to take Yi down and return him to the detention center. Yi and his wives and concubines all left with tears and dismay, quickly leaving.

### Student National Products Annual Meeting Holds Second Board Meeting Yesterday 154

Many Important Cases Passed

Shenshi News Agency reports that the Student National Products Promotion Federation held its second executive board meeting yesterday (the 15th) at the Shanghai Local Association on Jing'an Temple Road. More than ten people attended, including Pan Gongzhan, Huang Renzhi, and Zhu Xuefan. Many important cases were discussed and decided, and the meeting adjourned at about 8:00 PM. The details of each situation are recorded as follows.

Attendees

The Student National Products Year Promotion Federation held its second executive meeting at the Local Association at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The attending directors were Pan Gongzhan, Wu Zhihao, Yu Zuoting (represented by Zheng Chengqing), Huang Renzhi, Zhu Xuefan, Gu Yinqian, Chen Jicheng, Lin Kecong, Zheng Chengqing, Chu Fucheng, Yang Weiyu, Sun Daosheng (represented by Yang Weiyu), Zheng Xigu (represented by Yang Weiyu), Gu Jiwu, Fang Pixian (represented by Ying Zhengcang), Zai Jinping, Yang Jiaoqi, and more than ten others. The meeting was chaired by Pan Gongzhan and recorded by Yang Jiaoqi.

Resolutions

The cases resolved yesterday included: (1) What to do about Chen Guangfu's resignation as Chairman of the Economic Committee? It was resolved to retain him; (2) What to do about Mr. Liu Hongsheng and Wang Boqi's resignation as Economic Committee members? It was resolved to retain them; (3) The badge design should be specified. Resolved: Use a "heart" shape with the four characters "I use national products" in the middle, with the name of the association as the border; (4) Review and approve the nominations of the Design Committee for the Steering Committee. It was resolved to appoint Li Dachao as Honorary Secretary-General; (5) Formulate methods for raising advance funds. It was resolved to ask Yu Zuoting, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yansong, and the Local Association to provide temporary advances; (6) Review and approve the Student National Products Year song; (7) Revise and approve the detailed rules for the operation of the Cadre Department; (8) Revise and approve the solicitation of articles of association. The meeting was adjourned at about 8:00 PM.

Cat Skin and Fox Skin Listed as Special Light and Bulky Goods 155

The Two-Road Administration received instructions from the Ministry of Railways, stating that the Ping Sui Railway Administration telegraphed in December of the 23rd year, and the agency telegraphed No. 51 on the shimmering day of January of this year, stating that fur is a major commodity transported by the railway. It has always been charged as ordinary light and bulky goods. However, the volume per kilogram of this type of goods has actually exceeded four cubic decimeters. According to the charges for ordinary light and bulky goods, the burden on the merchants is too heavy. It is proposed to include all kinds of furs, except for wet hides, in the special light and bulky goods list, and collect freight at the rate of four cubic decimeters equivalent to one kilogram to reduce the burden on the merchants, etc., and attach a survey table of the volume and packaging of dry hides. According to this, after checking the various dry furs listed in the survey table, the degree of lightness and bulkiness varies. The current eleven items of overly light and bulky animal skin, cat skin, dog skin, sheep skin, fox skin, rabbit skin, gray mouse skin, wolf skin, leopard skin, marmot skin, and tiger skin are added to the list of special light and bulky goods and will be implemented from the 21st of this month. The remaining six items of mare skin, horse skin, cow skin, deer skin, and otter skin will still be charged freight as ordinary light and bulky goods. In addition to instructing and distributing, the bureau is ordered to comply with the instructions. The bureau has instructed the Vehicle Department to comply with the instructions.

Dr. Tang Jiazhen Announces the Principle of Egg Yolk Lecithin for Smoking Cessation 156

Yesterday, Dr. Tang Jiazhen announced the principle of egg lecithin for smoking cessation, saying that since Dr. Ma Wenzhao invented egg lecithin for smoking cessation, the Department of Health has adopted it to make smoking cessation medicines, which can be stopped immediately after smoking, without any pain, and the efficacy is remarkable and widely praised. The theory and principles of Dr. Ma are often scattered in various newspapers and magazines, but they are incomplete and not detailed enough, so that the general public cannot understand them. What we want to know is (1) the efficacy of egg yolk lecithin in smoking cessation, based on what kind of theory, (2) whether egg yolk lecithin is exclusively a smoking cessation medicine. According to Dr. Ma's years of research, the cells of human tissue contain a main part called the "Golgi body." This chemical component is a lipid, that is, egg yolk lecithin, etc. When the "Golgi body" in the cell increases, the person's spirit is invigorated, thoughts are renewed, and the limbs are used happily. Otherwise, the body is tired, the spirit is depressed, the whole body is sore and lazy, and there is no vitality. The function of opium is to stimulate the red blood cells in the blood to produce a large number of "platelets." The elements contained in platelets are nothing but lipids. Several kinds of white blood cells in the blood take this substance and transfer it to various organs, and the cells of each organ get this lipid, that is, to manufacture the "Golgi body" in its body. From this point of view, the Golgi body increased by opium is completely produced by its stimulating effect. After smoking for a long time, this kind of lipid cannot function without the power of opium. Therefore, when the opium addiction occurs, the number of platelets is greatly reduced, and the white blood cells stagnate in the blood vessels, not doing transportation work, and the cells of various organs naturally have no way to absorb this kind of lipid. As a result, the number of Golgi bodies that are originally there is greatly reduced or completely disappears, and all kinds of uneasy states appear, which is the so-called outbreak of smoking addiction. Egg yolk lecithin is a great tonic, and it is especially effective for smoking cessation in cases of neurasthenia and pulmonary tuberculosis. The reason is that its components are similar to the elements contained in platelets, because they are both lipids. After taking this element, white blood cells can directly take lipids from the intestines and send them to the cells of various organs. After the cells obtain this large amount of lipids and new troops, they can carry out their normal work, and they do not need to take it indirectly from red blood cells, so red blood cells can get rest and increase their effectiveness. During the period when we take egg lecithin, the Golgi body can directly take lipids from the intestine to increase its number, so we can get rid of the control of opium. Once the opium is reduced or even abandoned, the Golgi body is not in danger of disappearing because it has sufficient egg lecithin as its backing, and the purpose of physiological smoking cessation is achieved. Egg yolk lecithin can be obtained from three kinds of substances, one is animal brain, and the second is egg yolk lecithin in egg yolk, which Dr. Ma also believes is the best. According to the results of many scholars' experiments, egg lecithin is indeed a powerful tonic, as mentioned above. Even people who are not addicted to smoking can freely take it. Naturally, their weight will increase, their thinking will be quick, their complexion will be radiant, and there will be absolutely no elemental or any side effects. Therefore, egg lecithin is not only a smoking cessation product, but also an important tonic.

Xi Zhuping Invents Cultural Stove 161

The Ministry of Industry is Allowed to Patent for Five Years

A manufacturing factory will be established in Shanghai

Xi Pingzhu, a local industrial expert, has seen that our country's industry and commerce are backward, and the annual trade deficit is alarming, resulting in the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the depletion of people's livelihoods. In order to save rights and interests, he has invented a kind of cultural stove based on his research to resist foreign electric stoves. The outer shell of the stove is made of enamel. There is a stove hole on the upper left end, which can be used to put a pot for cooking. Below it is the stove door for lighting and extinguishing the fire. The edge of the stove hole is a water tank, which is connected to the right end with a tube. The steam is used to steam rice and stir-fry vegetables, so that rice, vegetables and other things can be completed at the same time. Each meal only costs one jiao for fuel. It is not only time-saving and cost-saving, but also very exquisite and beautiful. The size of the stove is divided into four types, and the highest selling price is set at nineteen yuan. The Ministry of Industry has allowed a patent for five years to promote it. It is heard that Mr. Xi intends to set up a manufacturing factory in Shanghai to meet social needs and produce as much as possible.

The "Zi Lin Bao" reports that Indian men Niaojiajia and Taila are accused of robbing the Dadong Tobacco Company of 7,544 yuan in wages on February 1st. After several hearings in the American Consulate's police court, a preliminary hearing was announced yesterday (the 14th). All three will be tried and convicted by the British Assize Court. As for the Chinese man who was shot in the left leg by the Indian man, according to doctors at Guangci Hospital yesterday, the bullet has been removed and he is expected to recover without any problems. It is said that if the bullet had been slightly more to the left, it would have been life-threatening, so he is fortunate.

Letter from the Fourth Branch of the Second Municipal Joint Association to the French Consul General

Requesting Correction of Erroneous Actions by Chinese Inspectors

The Fourth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Joint Association of Nanyang Bridge in the French Concession sent a letter to Mr. Gabriel, the French Chief of Police, yesterday, saying: "We are writing to you regarding a letter from Wang Lianqing of Wang Shunxing Woodware Shop at No. 206, Pingjili Road, a member of our association, stating that on the evening of the 12th of this month, around 8 pm, a large number of detectives from the French Concession police station suddenly came to the shop to search, claiming to be catching gamblers. At that time, four relatives of the shop's upstairs tenants, who were engaged in the old goods business, were gathering to play mahjong. After the detectives came upstairs, they found no gambling and told the four people that they could continue playing mahjong and did not arrest them. Then they went downstairs, and then went upstairs again, arresting all four people. They also dragged Wang Wenqing, an apprentice of our shop, who was already in bed downstairs, out of bed. The Chinese Inspector Qian Chenglong raised a handgun, aimed it at him, and threatened him to confess the gambling den. The apprentice did not know what was being asked and replied that he did not know. The inspector then began to beat him with fists and feet, arbitrarily assaulting him. Later, he was taken to the police station, where he was imprisoned, tortured, and threatened to confess that Mr. Dong Wenli was running a gambling den, in an attempt to falsely accuse a businessman. Inspector Qian said, 'You can say that Dong Wenli runs a gambling den, and I will release you.' The apprentice was young and, under such intimidation, could only answer 'yes.' It was not until the next day that everyone was released. We believe that gathering to play mahjong is a form of recreation and entertainment, which has always been allowed in the concession. We merchants do not understand the basis for the sudden arrival of the police detectives. After searching and finding nothing, and after the detectives allowed the four people to play mahjong, they arrested them again and went downstairs to drag the apprentice out of bed and torture him to confess. What crime did the apprentice commit to suffer such humiliation? According to the inspector's instigation, he pointed to Mr. Dong's gambling, which was a fabricated accusation. We merchants are at a loss to understand whether there is any personal animosity involved. Now our shop's apprentice is unwell due to the shock. Under such circumstances, how can we merchants conduct business? Therefore, we are reporting the facts to your association. At the same time, according to a letter from Mr. Dong Wenli, a standing committee member of our association, the police station sent detectives to search and monitor him. He is requesting that we find a way to negotiate this matter. Based on this, our association has conducted a detailed investigation. According to our association's standing committee member, Mr. Dong Wenli, he is indeed a legitimate businessman and has no illegal activities. This time, Inspector Qian's accusation of him gambling is completely unfounded and amounts to slander of a merchant's reputation and deliberate insult. Moreover, playing mahjong is a form of recreation and entertainment for merchants and citizens and is not prohibited by law. The inspector's repeated mistakes of detaining and assaulting people constitute an abuse of power and an infringement on the people's freedom. Therefore, after an emergency meeting of the executive committee of our association, it was decided that we should request your Consul General to thoroughly investigate the truth, correct the erroneous actions of the inspector, and guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future, in order to reassure the citizens and uphold the rule of law. We are sending this letter to you specifically, hoping that you will investigate and handle it, and give us a reply. February 15, 24th year of the Republic."

Civilian Sanatorium Expands Wards The Civilian Sanatorium at the intersection of Weihaiwei Road and Chongqing Road has been established for many years. The director, Yang Zhongfu, strives for perfection in the sanatorium's internal equipment. The chief physicians of various internal and external departments are all famous doctors. Therefore, the sanatorium's reputation has risen in recent years and has attracted the attention of the community. This is due to Director Yang's effective management. The sanatorium originally had dozens of wards. Because of the exquisite equipment and the fees being very suitable for the economic conditions of ordinary people, patients from the middle and upper classes have come from near and far, resulting in an insufficient number of wards. In view of this, the sanatorium has recently added several ordinary wards. The internal facilities are similar to those of the first and second-class wards, but the fees are several times lower. It has also hired more nurses, so that ordinary poor patients can enjoy the highest spiritual and material benefits at a small cost. Director Yang's dedication to helping the world can be seen from this. The sanatorium provides free diagnosis and medicine every day from 8:00 am to 10:00 am.

The Xujiahui Catholic Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that there are strong northerly seasonal winds around Shandong, the Yellow Sea, and North China. It is cloudy and cold, turning clear and bright later. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy and relatively cold, with fog on the coast. The northerly seasonal winds are quite strong, or there may be light rain. There is a light cyclone in the East China Sea, with fog in the northeast. The seasonal winds in the Taiwan Strait are intensifying. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 pm yesterday, the temperature in this city reached a maximum of 57.9 and a minimum of 36.5. On the same day last year, the maximum was 48.9 and the minimum was 23.4.

Business News

Financial Silver Prices Soar, Customs Gold Plummets Lowest Standard Gold Price at 917 Yuan 165

—Result: Another Drop of Seven Yuan—

The gold market yesterday saw overseas silver prices rise alarmingly, and the Central Bank's customs gold unit plummeted. Although public sentiment remained stable, sellers were more active and created a low price of 917 yuan. In the early morning, overseas silver markets in both England and the United States rose sharply, exchange rates contracted slightly, and although London gold rose by 2.5 pence, public sentiment was difficult to maintain. Preliminary trading outside the market opened and retreated to 22-23 yuan, then rose to 24 yuan. Unexpectedly, the Central Bank's listed prices were announced, with both England and the United States rising and the customs gold unit plummeting by 2.4%, pushing the standard gold price down to 953.6 yuan, rising and then falling again. After the opening, due to the lack of sellers from banks, swap transactions and long positions were squeezed, and forward exchange rates hardened again. Large traders came in and out again, sellers showed courage, lacked support, and retreated to within 20 yuan, creating a new low of 918 yuan. Banks then came to support, and prices rebounded. However, due to the HSBC listed price also rising, many parties were still panicked. Prices were high and then low, repeatedly rising and falling. The silver tax remained unchanged and had little impact. The situation revolved. Later, bank support became slightly stagnant, and the swap spread also dropped to about 12 yuan, allowing buyers to become active and prices to rise. Banks took advantage of the high prices to continue to supply, and the rise was blocked. Trading was light, and the situation was mediocre. Finally, the swap spread rose again to 13 yuan, and supply was relatively abundant. At noon, the market seemed tired, and the afternoon market was flat and tired, rising and falling uncertainly. Indian silver initially rose by 9 Anna and broke the 20 yuan mark, but buyers did not take it seriously, took advantage of the low prices to become active, and there was still a rebound. After entering the market, the swap spread became even higher, officially opening at 13.3 yuan from the short side, breaking the 20 yuan mark again. Although there was a struggle after entering the market, it was difficult to maintain due to the abundance of sellers. At this time, banks were eager to buy, and prices rebounded. After entering the market, the situation was still fierce, and although a price of 917 yuan was created again, Sassoon came to buy shillings, and buyers were agile, once rising to the 20 yuan mark. The market closed flat and tired. Throughout the day, due to the start of swap transactions, turnover seemed light, and the overall trend was confusing. The March to April term was traded with a short side spread of about 13 yuan. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opened at 922.4 yuan, down 3.3 yuan from the previous close. Fuchang entered orders, rising to 3.5 yuan. Fuxing, Yongzhao, Fengchang, Hengyu, and others competed to sell, falling to 19 yuan. China-Belgium Bank sold March US dollars at 1.25. Although Dalian and others took advantage of the low prices to enter at 20.03 yuan, it was difficult to sell March US dollars at 1.875, and Hengyu, Fuyu, Jiatai, Tongyu, Run, and others hurriedly sold, retreating to 18 yuan. Fuxing, Yongda, Dafayong, Wanxing, Tongyu Run, and others took advantage of the low prices to buy, returning to 252.5 yuan. It was learned that HSBC's listed price rose by 1.25 for British pounds and 0.20 for US dollars. Hengyu, Dayuan, Yifeng, Yong, and others sold, retreating to 0.08 yuan. If they were to release their positions slightly, those who follow the trend would inevitably cause a surge, and the manipulators would be hit. Apart from preparing funds to take delivery and gradually releasing the goods month by month, there is no other way to profit. All Remain Silent for Three Minutes to Commemorate the Deceased Budasen and Others

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) After several days of preparation, the 11th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Geological Society commenced today (the 14th) at 10:00 AM in the Geological Survey Institute Library. All directors were in attendance, except for Ding Wenjiang, who was delayed en route due to a freight train derailment in Weishanzhuang this morning. Over a hundred members from various regions were also present, including Sked from Qilu University, Long Xiangqi, Director of the Xujiahui Observatory, and Wang Gongmu, Director of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau. Details from various parties are recorded as follows:

Grand Opening

Chairman Xie Jiarong delivered the opening address, stating that the meeting was originally scheduled to be held in the newly completed Geology Museum at Peking University. However, due to unfinished internal construction, it was moved to the Ping Institute Library. The society has a history of thirteen years, but two annual meetings were not held, making this the eleventh. A major highlight of this year's meeting is the awarding of the Grabau Medal. This medal was established by Grabau in 1925, and only the deceased Budasen and others have received it. However, the two individuals to whom the medal should be awarded today are not present, and their names will be temporarily preserved. Xie continued, stating that member Long Xiangqi, Director of the Xujiahui Observatory, accompanied Chairman Chiang Kai-shek on an inspection of the Northwest and took extremely valuable films from the plane, as well as presentations on the stratigraphy of both sides of the Yellow River and the geology of Ningxia, either through slides or film screenings. He hoped everyone would pay attention.

Reports

(1) Secretary of the General Assembly Sun Yunzhu reported on the loss of members in the past year and a half. According to statistics, Budasen and three others passed away in the past year and a half. (2) Qian Shengjun reported on the financial situation. (3) Weng Wenhao reported on editing matters, which was announced and approved for record by all members. (4) Wang Gongmu, Director of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, stood up and gave a very detailed report on the progress of scientific terminology. However, the matter is of great importance, and the efforts of the masses cannot form a solid wall, so he hoped that the Geological Society would provide assistance and jointly review it, as this issue is related to the development of science education in China and is extremely important in academic terms. Weng Wenhao and Sked then successively expressed their opinions.

Memorial Service for Deceased Members

The chairman then proposed that all members observe one minute of silence for the deceased members to express their condolences. This was unanimously agreed upon, and everyone stood and remained silent for three minutes. The meeting place was immediately quiet and solemn. At this point, the business meeting of the 11th Annual Meeting of the Geological Society was declared closed, and films were then shown, including stratigraphy of the Yellow River basin, and conditions in Ningxia province. The showing ended around 12 o'clock, and a photo break was taken.

Chinese Iron Ore

Xie Jiarong read the paper "Classification of Chinese Iron Ore" at 2:00 PM. The gist of it was as follows: The classification method of Chinese iron ore presented this time refers to the latest ore deposit theory, with genesis as the main factor and the type, age, and deposition method of the ore-bearing layer as secondary factors, divided into five major categories and seventeen types. Each type is named after a place name, such as the Shanxi type and the Xuanlong type. According to Xie's classification method, expert Grabau expressed his approval on the spot.

New Mineral Discovery

Wang Zuoquan announced the paper "Research on Tin Arsenic Ore in Hunan" at 2:40 PM. The main points of his discovery are as follows: The Hunan ore deposit occurs in the Carboniferous limestone and is very close to granite. The collected specimens were polished into smooth surfaces and thin sections, placed under reflective and transmissive microscopes for separate examination. As a result, the main minerals found were arsenopyrite, cassiterite, pyrite, chalcopyrite, sphalerite, stannite, magnetite, pyrite, bornite, chalcocite, enargite, and other detailed examination of the order of deposition of each mineral ore, the relationship between primary and secondary, and the presumed formation of cylindrical ore deposits. It seems that the ore deposited earlier first constitutes the circular outer ring, which is then filled with the minerals deposited later.

Ore Deposits Discovered

Zhu Xiren read the paper "Genesis of Copper Deposits in Western Sichuan" at 3:30 PM. His new discoveries are as follows: (1) Copper ore in basalt is widely distributed in western Sichuan. Its genesis is all attributed to the influence of post-eruption effects. At that time, the temperature should be below 250 degrees Celsius. The source of its sulfide ore should be agglomerated from the basalt body itself. (2) Sedimentary copper ore is located in the coal-bearing rock at the bottom of the Triassic strata. The negative rock is directly located on the secondary Triassic basalt. The genesis of this type of copper ore is that during the Triassic period, this estuary or marine sediment's coast was formed by secondary Triassic basalt. Copper ore from basalt is weathered into copper sulfate liquid.

Granite Metamorphism

Yang Jie announced the paper "Metamorphism Around the Yangfang Granite in the Western Hills of Beiping" at 4:00 PM. His new discoveries are as follows: Between Yangfang, Dajuesi, and Wenquan in the Western Hills of Beiping, there is a large granite outcrop. This rock was obstructed by the orogenic movement in the early Cenozoic era. Because of its relatively new age, the ages of the various strata connected to it are also very complicated. In the north, west of Yangfang, this granite is in contact with volcanic rock layers. In a certain location of Jufeng Dajuesi, there is also a layer of shale between the granite and the volcanic rock. In Nan'anhe Wenquan and other places, the granite is in contact with metamorphic limestone. Above this limestone, there is a thick layer of shale, which is commonly seen in Jufeng Dajuesi and other places. The Chengzi Mountain and Shijingshan mountain ranges are entirely made of this rock. Above this thick shale is the coal system, followed by thick sandstone shale, followed by intrusive rock, and the uppermost is shale, sandstone, gravel, etc. These strata have undergone metamorphism due to the granite magma. From this metamorphism, various metamorphic minerals were regenerated. The geological structure here is also quite interesting. The northern granite directly fills the upper volcanic rock layer, the western part fills the lower shale layer above the volcanic rock, and the southern part only reaches the lower Paleozoic limestone. Therefore, this ah limestone should be Cambrian and Ordovician, and the shale above it should be the Jiulongshan series. The shale between Dajuesi and Jufeng should be contemporaneous. Also, south of Chengshan, due to faults, the Mei system (should be the Yangjiatun system) overlies Jiulong. Because at the uppermost part of this coal, there is the Jiulongshan series. In addition, in Wenquan East, Heilongtan and other places, the coal system is in direct contact with wood ash rock, which can prove that from the south of Chengzi Mountain to Heilongtan there is a fault. There should be more springs in this fault, but on the line of Jinshan Dajuesi, the springs should have another origin and should not be confused. This is because the upper part is a volcanic rock layer, which receives seepage and flows downwards, flows to the upper surface of the lower granite, and then flows out.

Orthoclase Quartz

Chen Guoyuan read the paper "Orthoclase Quartzite of Ma'anshan, East of Rongcheng County, Shandong" at 5:45 PM. The gist is as follows: The geology of Rongcheng County can be said to have not been well studied until now. Now only a simple study of the geology of Ma'anshan in the southeast is presented. This mountain has two peaks, named for its saddle-like shape. The lower layer in its western part is a most interesting orthoclase rock. This rock is mostly composed of orthoclase, and between these minerals, there are many quartz, hornblende microcrystals. Above this orthoclase rock is the upper trachyte, and above that is rhyolite. Therefore, it can be inferred that the age of this rock is the most recent, or it may be similar to the alkaline orthoclase rocks in Linxian, Shanxi. Chen finished reading the paper at 6:40 PM. The chairman announced the adjournment of the meeting and that the meeting would continue tomorrow (the 15th) with public lectures in the morning and papers read in the afternoon. (14th)

(Nanjing, 15th) The Ministry of Education, in accordance with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, believes that the fisheries industry in China has become important in recent years and that there is a lack of fisheries talent. The Central Government Formulates Educational Measures for Descendants of Confucius 182

The educational measures for the descendants of Confucius were jointly reviewed by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education and submitted to the Central Government for approval. Each person admitted to a university will be given 800 yuan, and each person admitted to a secondary school will be given 400 yuan, but only the direct descendants of the four surnames Kong, Yan, Zeng, and Meng (Confucius, Yan Hui, Zeng Shen, and Mencius) are eligible. In addition, for primary school education, a survey will first be conducted to determine whether primary school education has been established in Qufu, Shandong. If there are primary schools for the descendants of the four surnames Kong, Yan, Zeng, and Meng, subsidies will be provided to expand enrollment. If no primary school has been established, another plan will be made to establish one to achieve more. The Ministry of Education has ordered the Shandong Education Department to conduct a close and thorough investigation of the current number of descendants of Confucius in Qufu, as well as the detailed situation of how many people can enter universities or secondary schools, in order to plan. It is also heard that during the investigation, the Lu Education Department will be asked to find out how many descendants of the four surnames Kong, Yan, Zeng, and Meng there are in total, their level of education, where the four surnames live, and whether there are any public or private primary schools or public buildings that can be used for schools. All details will be reported.

Shanghai University Federation Advocates Proper Entertainment for Students 187

Art Research Set as Extracurricular Work

Assist Students in Organizing Art Research Associations

Since banning students from dancing, the Shanghai University Federation has taken a step further to advocate proper entertainment for students. At the first general meeting of this year, the proposal to promote proper entertainment, proposed by the presidents of Jiaotong University and the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts, was passed and sent to all universities for implementation. Details are recorded as follows:

Reasons for Advocacy

In recent times, general schools lack guidance in spiritual life, and students have no proper entertainment outside of class to regulate their minds. Although the previous resolution of this meeting to ban dancing was to correct the students' habits, it was not what was intended without guidance in the active aspect. My colleagues and others have based on the resolutions of the Executive Committee, proposed that schools organize art research associations to be a proper extracurricular activity for students, which can not only cultivate temperament, improve students' interests, cultivate a solemn school group, but also promote the glory of China's inherent culture, search for the elite of foreign art studies, integrate them, and lay the foundation for a new culture.

Implementation Methods

(1) Schools should jointly organize extracurricular calligraphy, painting, epigraphy, poetry, children's music, drama, photography, and other research associations by teachers and students in each college or grade. (2) The above research associations should be designated as extracurricular work by schools in the school rules, and the school authorities should vigorously promote and assist. (3) The research associations should set up research and administrative departments. The research department should be divided into research, lecture, editing, visit, and exhibition groups, and the administrative department should be divided into document, accounting, general affairs, and communication groups, which should be taken care of by members. (4) The research associations should be held regularly and experts from inside and outside the school should be invited to guide or lecture. (5) Research associations, competitions, review meetings, exhibitions, concerts, and federations of various schools should be used to connect feelings and learn from each other. (6) The organizational charter of the research association will be formulated separately.

Circular to Various Schools

The association sent a letter to various universities in the city, saying, "Respectfully, the first general meeting of the 23rd year resolved to promote the use of domestic products and sent a circular to various schools to promote them as much as possible. Domestic products should be selected for stationery and provincial examinations. The proposal to promote savings among faculty and staff was resolved to be sent to various schools to seek opinions. As for the proposal to promote proper entertainment, it was resolved to ask schools to organize art research associations and send the proposals of Jiaotong University, Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts, and Tongji University to various schools for reference."

Organizations Springing Up

Since the advocacy, various schools have organized one after another. The methods of Jiaotong University and Tongji University are recorded below. (A) Jiaotong University supplements the method of promoting proper entertainment for students. (1) Ask various music schools to hold concerts regularly. (2) Ask various art schools to hold art exhibitions regularly. (3) Organize holiday trips and weekend trips. (4) Hold valuable and interesting movies. (5) Exchange various entertainment performances between universities. (6) Organize research associations for calligraphy, painting, and photography. (7) Organize rowing boat competitions. (B) Tongji University's proposed proper entertainment methods are as follows. Organize art research associations, which are initiated by students from each school, and teachers and staff with artistic skills and interests are invited to participate. The association charter is formulated and meetings are held regularly, or exhibitions are opened for people to read in order to learn from each other. As for the types of art research, they can be divided into the above several types. (1) Painting. (2) Calligraphy. (3) Photography. (4) Sculpture.

Special Article

What College Graduates Should Know About Serving in the Banking Industry 191

— Tang Shoumin

The following is an address by Mr. Tang Shoumin, General Manager of the Bank of Communications, to the special probationary employees:

Gentlemen, it has been three or four months since you joined the bank. I have been too busy with affairs to meet with you. Today, I am taking the opportunity to talk to you, firstly to get to know everyone, and secondly to express my hopes for you. Now, let me start by talking about the history of our bank.

The Bank of Communications was established in the 33rd year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty with the approval of the Ministry of Posts and Communications, as a joint government-private venture. It was stipulated that in addition to ordinary banking business, all funds related to the four major administrations—postal, shipping, telegraph, and railway—would be managed by our bank. Hence the name "Communications." At that time, the nature of our bank's business was truly a specialized bank with a dedicated mission. This can be considered the "first period" in the history of our bank. In the third year of the Republic of China, the President promulgated the Regulations of the Bank of Communications, stipulating that in addition to ordinary business, the bank was permitted to manage special accounting funds of the national treasury and had the right to manage national treasury bonds and issue convertible notes. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, a general sub-branch for regional issuance was established, specializing in the preparation of publicly independent issuances. Later, after various changes and numerous replacements, the period was very long. This can be considered the "second period" in the history of our bank. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the principles were changed, and the National Government announced conditions to make our bank a national industrial development bank, setting the business term to thirty years. Thus, our bank re-specified the undertaking of various businesses, and the head office was also moved to Shanghai at that time. At that time (the eighteenth year of the Republic of China), I took office as the manager of the Shanghai branch, determined to operate diligently to promote development. This can be considered the "third period" in the history of our bank.

Now, I am back to serve the Bank of Communications, overseeing the overall bank affairs. I originally hoped to "make waves within the established framework." Unfortunately, the world economic situation is unfavorable, the rural economy is bankrupt, and natural and man-made disasters have followed one after another. The situation is different, the environment is complex, and the original plan may not be achieved immediately. We can only be determined, work hard, and eventually achieve our goals. We will discuss this matter next time.

In the past, the bank's personnel system emphasized emotions. Because the recommendation system was used, relatives and friends could be introduced. I dare not say that all the colleagues who came in through the recommendation system were bad, but at least I can say that this kind of recommendation system is absolutely unsuitable for today's evolving society. Furthermore, if I have relatives who are officials, then I can also become an official. This kind of bad situation is one of the major reasons for the lack of progress in various Chinese enterprises. The prosperity of all undertakings depends entirely on talent. Without talent, there is no enterprise. Even if an enterprise can be barely maintained, it is not easy to develop. I often lament that there are many idle people in society, and the authorities lament the difficulty of finding talent. This phenomenon is indeed a current situation in Chinese society. Some people often say that this is all due to the bad recommendation system, but I deeply sympathize with this situation. Therefore, to change this system, there is nothing better than examinations and selections, and the method of recommending outstanding graduates from universities. I feel especially gratified to be talking to you today.

I do not talk about personal feelings, nor do I advocate recommendations. I use screening methods and examination systems to select outstanding talents. This is not only a first for our bank but also rare among our counterparts. Therefore, I have great expectations for you and feel a very urgent need. In recent years, the banking industry has gradually become more specialized and technical. Those engaged in banking must not only have the skills of calculating accounts and the experience of bookkeeping but also have legal knowledge, scientific methods, and applied technology to improve efficiency. For investments in the industrial sector, specialized talent is even more needed for investigation and research. Therefore, your arrival here is partly a supplement to the bank's need for talent and partly a response to the need for specialized knowledge. Although you are currently ordinary bank staff, you will all be the backbone of the bank in the future. Therefore, you must understand the importance of your position and realize the vastness of your future.

When you leave school life and enter society, you should always remember that the first thing is to read, the second is to gain experience, and the third is to determine your work direction and become a well-rounded talent. This kind of well-rounded talent is not only for our bank; in a few years, we hope to produce many managerial talents for the banking industry and create many general manager talents. This is my fundamental principle of cultivating and cherishing talent.

In terms of work, some people used to advocate that good performers should stay and bad performers should be returned to their schools. This kind of policy should be the case in terms of employing people. But now, after reading your internship reports from various departments, most of them are not bad, and some are excellent. I can say that all of you can stay, and the official announcement has already been made. We will assess your work performance again and promote those with excellent performance at any time. Those who are not performing well will still have screening days. You should pay special attention.

Secondly, I am here working with you all, and everyone should serve the bank with all their energy. Everyone should understand each other's situation. Now, let me introduce my experience to you. I am neither a college graduate nor a middle school graduate. I came from a money shop and reached this position entirely through experience. I have worked in accounting, business, cashiering, and documentation. I have also been the manager of small and large banks. My environment has involved perseverance, hard work, striving, patience, etc. From the late Qing Dynasty to the Republic of China, there is nearly 30 years of history. Even if the late Qing Dynasty is not counted, there are already 23 years of relations with the financial world. Therefore, to have considerable success, there must be considerable effort and time. You have just left school and do not need to be overly eager for quick success. You have now been assigned to various positions, including eleven in the audit department, four in the business department, six in the business research office, and one in the savings and credit department. This is the beginning of serving the bank. But how your future will be depends on your efforts. Now, let me tell you what I hope for you. Please pay attention.

(1) Patience: The most important thing when serving society is to endure hardship and work hard. When encountering unsatisfactory things, you should be patient. Even if you are wronged temporarily, someone will eventually see it. When you are dissatisfied with the bank's affairs, do not be polite. Use legal procedures to state your opinions. Now, we must break bad habits and not have class concepts. If there is not enough time for a face-to-face conversation, or if there is no time for a face-to-face conversation, you can use communication methods to explain. I am very willing to accept your opinions and will never subject you to any grievances.

American Athlete Invents Butterfly Swimming Style 193

Breaks World Record

Tokyo, Japan, 15th dispatch from the Japanese Press Association: American swimmer John Higgins created a new record of 1 minute and 11.8 seconds for the 100-meter breaststroke at a competition on January 13, breaking the previous world record of 1 minute and 12.4 seconds held by a French athlete. The swimming style used by Higgins is the so-called butterfly stroke (Bettergby), which is newly popular in the United States. This record confirms the advantages of this swimming style. It is expected to revolutionize the world of swimming. If this swimming style demonstrates its power in the future, Japan must also study it. The butterfly stroke involves extending both hands forward in the water during the breaststroke. However, this method lifts both hands out of the water to the side and then moves them forward, making it very fast. Its appearance is like a butterfly flapping its wings, hence the name.

Shanghai Basketball Association Daily Report 194

Xinguang Wins Against Zhongshe (Group B2): 38 to 21

Zhenru Wins Against Dongya (Group AA): 41 to 23

Haizei Wins Against Jiangwan (Group AA): 55 to 39

Maijin Wins Against Yingdui (Group AA): 60 to 43

The Shanghai Basketball Association had three Group AA games last night, one after another. Zhenru, Haizei, and Maijin won, while Dongya, Jiangwan, and Yingdui were defeated. However, the performances of Jiangwan and Yingdui can be considered excellent in the first half of the games. Unfortunately, they could not persevere to the end. The situations of the three matches are described on the left.

Zhenru Wins Against Dongya

In the battle between the two armies, Dongya took the lead with 4 to 0. The Zhenru players calmly faced the battle and gradually caught up and surpassed them. Afterwards, Dongya was too eager to win, which led to the situation of wanting to achieve quick success but not achieving it. As a result, Zhenru won with a score of 41 to 23.

Haizei Defeats Jiangwan

Jiangwan's soldiers cautiously approached the enemy, making the tenacious Haizei unable to act fiercely for a time. They also took the lead with scores of 8 to 4 and 10 to 6, occupying the peak for ten minutes. The Haizei was in a precarious situation. Smith replaced Klaus, and Jiangwan suffered from it. Despite their efforts to resist, they were able to equalize twice at 14 to 16. This was the golden age of Jiangwan's overall game. In the second half, the Haizei became even more rampant. The defensive power of this side gradually weakened, resulting in an irrecoverable battle. After fighting for forty minutes, they were defeated by the Haizei with a score of 55 to 39.

Maijin Defeats Yingdui

The entire Yingdui army embraced the determination to fight to the death, determined to fight the brave Maijin. After the start, they played vividly, once occupying an absolute advantage with a score of 12 to 2. However, the opponents were tall and strong, and they were able to catch up. By the end of the first half, they reversed the score with 26 to 24 and took the lead by one point. In the second half, Yingdui was still able to hold on for ten minutes, but afterwards, they felt that their hearts were strong but their strength was insufficient, and they had to admit defeat.
